              <h1 class="uppercase" style="font-family: Lora;">
               JEWELRY &amp; ACCESSORIES WITH CHARACTER HANDCRAFTED FOR YOU
              </h1>
              <p class="color_444 fs_lg">
               Embark in a time travel with jewelry and accessories as your guide. Let yourself immerse into cultures dating from five thousand years ago by exploring pieces either inspired by the ancient original ones or identical to the prototypes.
              </p>
              <p class="color_444 fs_lg">
               Get the feeling, the symbolism, the simplicity or the opulence they bring with them, their fusion with contemporary designs and influences and their evolution. Keep a taste of this journey with a handcrafted piece made for you.
              </p>
              <p class="color_444 fs_lg">
              </p>
